‚óè Ah! I found the issue! Looking at the model, ChatMessageResponse expects sender_type and message_type to be SenderType and MessageType enum values (lines 36, 39), but the
  database stores them as strings.

  When creating the ChatMessageResponse from the database row (line 79 in chat.py: ChatMessageResponse(**msg)), Pydantic is trying to validate the string values from the database
  against the Enum types, which might be failing.

  Let me check the actual database schema to see what values are stored:

‚óè Bash(mysql -h camerascasas.no-ip.info -P 3308 -u producao -p112358123 langnet -e "SELECT sender_type, message_type FROM chat_messages WHERE session_id = '9f587efb-b9‚Ä¶)
  ‚éø ¬†sender_type	message_typ
     agent	progress
     user	chat
     system	status

‚óè The values look correct. But wait, let me check if the model is using str type with Enum constraint correctly. Looking at line 11-16 and 19-28, the enums inherit from str and
  Enum, which should allow string values to work. But Pydantic might be strict about case sensitivity.

  Actually, looking more carefully at the model, the issue is that SenderType and MessageType use uppercase enum values (USER, AGENT, SYSTEM, CHAT, STATUS, etc.) but the database
  has lowercase values (user, agent, system, chat, status, etc.).

  This is the bug! The enum values in the model don't match the case of the values in the database. Let me fix this:

     ‚ö†Ô∏è Pontos de Aten√ß√£o

     1. API Keys: Precisa ter OPENAI_API_KEY ou DEEPSEEK_API_KEY no .env
     2. Custo: Chamadas LLM podem ser caras com documentos grandes
     3. Tempo: An√°lise completa pode levar 2-5min por documento
     4. Weasyprint: Pode precisar instalar depend√™ncias do sistema (libpango, etc.)

     - ‚úÖ Upload de documentos

     - ‚úÖ Renderiza√ß√£o markdown no chat

     üöÄ Resultado Final

     Sistema completo onde usu√°rio:
     1. Faz upload de RFP/documentos
     2. IA analisa e gera requisitos markdown
     3. V√™ requisitos no chat
     4. Edita manualmente se quiser

     7. IA refina baseado em vers√£o original OU editada
     8. Exporta PDF profissional
     9. Todo hist√≥rico salvo no banco

     Tudo integrado, funcional e pronto para produ√ß√£o!

        25 +  async def execute_analysis_in_background(
        26 +      session_id: str,
        27 +      execution_id: str,
        28 +      project_id: str,
        29 +      documents: list,
        30 +      instructions: str,
        31 +      use_web_research: bool
        32 +  ):
        33 +      """
        34 +      Execute LangNet analysis in background and save results
        35 +      """
        36 +      try:
        37 +          # Send progress updates via WebSocket
        38 +          await connection_manager.broadcast_to_execution(
        39 +              execution_id,
        40 +              {"type": "task_started", "task": "document_analysis", "message": "Iniciando an√°lise com IA..."}
        41 +          )
        42 +  
        43 +          # For now, we'll process the first document
        44 +          # TODO: Support multiple documents analysis
        45 +          doc_id, doc_filename, doc_path = documents[0]
        46 +  
        47 +          # Execute LangNet workflow
        48 +          result_state = execute_document_analysis_workflow(
        49 +              project_id=project_id,
        50 +              document_id=doc_id,
        51 +              document_path=doc_path,
        52 +              additional_instructions=instructions,
        53 +              enable_web_research=use_web_research
        54 +          )
        55 +  
        56 +          # Extract requirements document
        57 +          requirements_doc = result_state.get('requirements_document_md', '')
        58 +  
        59 +          # Save to database
        60 +          with get_db_connection() as conn:
        61 +              cursor = conn.cursor()
        62 +              cursor.execute("""
        63 +                  UPDATE execution_sessions
        64 +                  SET requirements_document = %s, status = 'completed', finished_at = NOW()
        65 +                  WHERE id = %s
        66 +              """, (requirements_doc, session_id))
        67 +              conn.commit()
        68 +              cursor.close()
        69 +  
        70 +          # Send completion message
        71 +          save_chat_message(
        72 +              session_id=session_id,
        73 +              sender_type='agent',
        74 +              message_text='‚úÖ An√°lise conclu√≠da! Documento de requisitos gerado.',
        75 +              message_type='result',
        76 +              task_execution_id=None,
        77 +              sender_name='Agente Analista',
        78 +              metadata={'execution_id': execution_id, 'has_document': True}
        79 +          )
        80 +  
        81 +          # Send document as separate message
        82 +          save_chat_message(
        83 +              session_id=session_id,
        84 +              sender_type='agent',
        85 +              message_text=requirements_doc,
        86 +              message_type='document',
        87 +              task_execution_id=None,
        88 +              sender_name='Agente Analista',
        89 +              metadata={'execution_id': execution_id, 'document_type': 'requirements'}
        90 +          )
        91 +  
        92 +          await connection_manager.broadcast_to_execution(
        93 +              execution_id,
        94 +              {"type": "execution_completed", "message": "An√°lise conclu√≠da!", "session_id": session_id}
        95 +          )
        96 +  
        97 +      except Exception as e:
        98 +          print(f"‚ùå Error in background analysis: {e}")
        99 +          import traceback
       100 +          traceback.print_exc()
       101 +  
       102 +          # Update status to failed
       103 +          with get_db_connection() as conn:
       104 +              cursor = conn.cursor()
       105 +              cursor.execute("""
       106 +                  UPDATE execution_sessions
       107 +                  SET status = 'failed', finished_at = NOW()
       108 +                  WHERE id = %s
       109 +              """, (session_id,))
       110 +              conn.commit()
       111 +              cursor.close()
       112 +  
       113 +          # Send error message
       114 +          save_chat_message(
       115 +              session_id=session_id,
       116 +              sender_type='system',
       117 +              message_text=f'‚ùå Erro na an√°lise: {str(e)}',
       118 +              message_type='error',
       119 +              task_execution_id=None,
       120 +              metadata={'execution_id': execution_id, 'error': str(e)}
       121 +          )
       122 +  
       123 +          await connection_manager.broadcast_to_execution(
       124 +              execution_id,
       125 +              {"type": "execution_failed", "error": str(e)}
       126 +          )
       127 +

     Arquivo: backend/app/routers/documents.py:48-54

     Problema: 
     # Linha 48 - ERRADO: Chamada S√çNCRONA em contexto ASYNC
     result_state = execute_document_analysis_workflow(...)

     Explica√ß√£o:
     - Fun√ß√£o execute_analysis_in_background() √© async
     - Dentro dela, chama LangNet que √© S√çNCRONO e demora 2-5min

     - Por isso parece "instant√¢neo" - √© um bug, n√£o resposta real

     üîß CORRE√á√ïES A FAZER

     Corre√ß√£o #1: Executar LangNet em Thread Separada

     Arquivo: backend/app/routers/documents.py

     Linha 48, MUDAR DE:
     result_state = execute_document_analysis_workflow(
         project_id=project_id,
         document_id=doc_id,
         document_path=doc_path,
         additional_instructions=instructions,
         enable_web_research=use_web_research
     )

     PARA:
     # Executar workflow bloqueante em thread pool (n√£o bloqueia event loop)
     result_state = await asyncio.to_thread(
         execute_document_analysis_workflow,
         project_id=project_id,
         document_id=doc_id,
         document_path=doc_path,
         additional_instructions=instructions,
         enable_web_research=use_web_research
     )

     Resultado:
     - ‚úÖ Workflow executa em thread separada
     - ‚úÖ N√£o bloqueia event loop async
     - ‚úÖ Demora 2-5 minutos como esperado
     - ‚úÖ WebSocket envia atualiza√ß√µes em tempo real

     Corre√ß√£o #3: Limpar Dados de Teste

     -- Limpar sess√µes de teste antigas
     DELETE FROM execution_sessions 
     WHERE status = 'completed' 
       AND requirements_document IS NOT NULL
       AND started_at < NOW() - INTERVAL 1 HOUR;

     -- OU manter apenas sess√µes recentes
     UPDATE execution_sessions 
     SET requirements_document = NULL
     WHERE id NOT IN (
       SELECT id FROM execution_sessions 
       ORDER BY started_at DESC 
       LIMIT 5
     );

     ---
     ‚ö†Ô∏è NOTAS IMPORTANTES

     Por que o Bug Aconteceu:

     async def execute_analysis_in_background(...):  # ‚Üê fun√ß√£o async
         # ...
         result_state = execute_document_analysis_workflow(...)  # ‚Üê chamada S√çNCRONA
         # ^ Isso BLOQUEIA o event loop inteiro!

     Python permite isso mas √© anti-pattern. O correto √©:
     async def execute_analysis_in_background(...):
         result_state = await asyncio.to_thread(  # ‚Üê executa em thread
             execute_document_analysis_workflow, ...
         )

     Tempo Esperado de An√°lise:

     - Sem web research: 1-2 minutos
     - Com web research: 3-5 minutos
     - Depende de: Tamanho do documento, modelo LLM usado

     - ‚úÖ DeepSeek (deepseek-chat)
     - ‚úÖ Serper (web research)
     - ‚úÖ SerpAPI (fallback)

     Ap√≥s as corre√ß√µes:
